<div class=WordSection2>

<h1 style='margin-top:0in'><a name="_Toc134528011"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>PROMULGATION STATEMENT</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>The mission of the Training and Leader Development
Division (TLDD) of the Texas Department of Criminal Justice (TDCJ) is to
recruit and retain correctional officers, provide quality training, develop
leadership capacity, and promote a healthy workforce in order to inspire
confidence and retain employees. To accomplish this mission, the TLDD must
ensure its operations are performed efficiently with minimal disruption,
especially during an emergency. This document provides planning and program
guidance for implementing the TLDD Continuity of Operations Plan and programs
to ensure the division <span class=GramE>is capable of conducting</span> its
essential missions and functions under all threats and conditions.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Key TLDD personnel who are relocated under this plan
are collectively known as Continuity Personnel. Upon Plan activation, these
members will deploy to a designated location, establish an operational
capability, and perform Essential Functions within 12 hours from the time of
the activation of the Continuity Plan, for up to a 30-day period or until
normal operations can be resumed.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>The Continuity Director for the TLDD is the division
director or their designated successor. The Continuity Director serves as the
overall authority for Continuity planning and operations for the TLDD during a
Continuity event. The Continuity Director is responsible for ensuring the
continuation of Essential Functions and operations.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>This plan has been developed to meet the standards
of the FEMA Continuity of Operations planning model as outlined in the Texas
Continuity Template, Texas Labor Code 412.054, Texas House Bill 1832 and the
Texas Continuity Policy Letters (2013 and 2019) as well as FEMA Continuity
Guidance Circular (2018).<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_1" o:spid="_x0000_s2050"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='position:absolute;margin-left:238.7pt;margin-top:8.85pt;

 mso-wrap-distance-left:9pt;mso-wrap-distance-top:0;mso-wrap-distance-right:9pt;
 mso-wrap-distance-bottom:0;mso-position-horizontal:absolute;
 mso-position-horizontal-relative:margin;mso-position-vertical:absolute;
 mso-position-vertical-relative:text;mso-width-percent:0;mso-height-percent:0;
 mso-width-relative:margin;mso-height-relative:margin'>
 <v:imagedata src="TLDD%20COOP_files/image003.png" o:title=""/>
 <w:wrap anchorx="margin"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><span style='mso-ignore:vglayout;position:
absolute;z-index:-1895825408;margin-left:405px;margin-top:333px;width:350px;
height:108px'><img width=280 height=86 src="TLDD%20COOP_files/image004.png"
v:shapes="Picture_x0020_1"></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=right style='text-align:right'><span style='font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:3.0in;mso-add-space:auto;tab-stops:6.5in'><u><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'> </span><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:3.0in;mso-add-space:auto'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>David Yebra,
Director VI<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:3.0in;mso-add-space:auto'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>Division Director
<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:3.0in;mso-add-space:auto'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>Training and
Leader Development Division <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;
margin-left:3.0in;mso-add-space:auto'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'>September 1, 2023<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-top:0in;
mso-margin-bottom-alt:6.0pt;mso-margin-top-alt:0in;mso-add-space:auto;
text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc134528012"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>CONFIDENTIALITY
STATEMENT</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>This Continuity Plan is confidential.
Portions of this Continuity Plan contain information that raises personal
privacy or other concerns, and those portions may be exempt from mandatory
disclosure under the Public Information Act of Texas. It is to be controlled,
stored, handled, transmitted, distributed, and disposed of in accordance with
Executive Directive ED-02.29 Records Management and is not to be released to
the public or other personnel who do not have a valid need to know without
prior approval of the TLDD director.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>Some of the information in this Plan,
if made public, could endanger the lives and privacy of employees. In addition,
the disclosure of information in this Plan could compromise the security of
essential equipment, services, and systems of the TLDD or otherwise impair its
ability to carry out Essential Functions. Distribution of the Continuity Plan
in whole or in part is limited to those personnel who need to know the
information in order to successfully implement the Plan.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>The TLDD Office of Information
Management will distribute copies of the Continuity Plan on a need-to-know basis.
Requests for copies of the Plan shall be submitted from the applicable
department manager to the manager of Training and Support Operations for
approval. In addition, copies of the Plan will be distributed to other
organizations as necessary to promote information sharing and facilitate a
coordinated interagency Continuity effort. Further distribution of the Plan, in
hardcopy or electronic form, is not allowed without approval from the TLDD
director. The TLDD Office of Information Management will distribute updated
versions of the Continuity Plan annually or as critical changes occur.</span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
color:#44546A;mso-themecolor:text2;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
</span></b>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Montserrat;color:#44546A;mso-themecolor:
text2'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<w:Sdt SdtDocPart="t" DocPartType="Table of Contents" DocPartUnique="t"
 ID="-199711655">
 <p class=MsoTocHeading><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Table of Contents<o:p></o:p></span><span

<h1 style='margin-top:0in'><a name="_Toc134528013"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>ESSENTIAL FUNCTIONS</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'>Using CGC guidance, the </span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>organization has
identified its<b> </b>EFs, a limited set of its overall functions that must be
continued throughout, or resumed rapidly after, a disruption of normal
activities. These EFs have been approved by </span><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>the Training and Leader Development Division director<b> </b><span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>are listed below in priority order.<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='margin-top:0in'><a name="_Toc134528014"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>ESSENTIAL RECORDS</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528015"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Identification
and Storage</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>The TLDD Office of
Information Management</span><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial'> <span style='color:black'>maintains a complete inventory of essential records,
along with their locations and instructions for access</span></span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

  0in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Montserrat'>IBM Backup<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=120 style='width:1.25in;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  Audits Monthly<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:6;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;page-break-inside:avoid'>

<h2><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528016"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Backup and Protection</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'>Electronic records, and the records
inventory, are backed-up by the Information Technology Division. If they are
lost, recovery will be conducted by the Information Technology Division.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
color:black;mso-themecolor:text1'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528017"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Recovery</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Recovery
is expensive, time consuming, and may not be completely effective, so every
effort should be made to prevent damage to essential records. If essential
records are damaged, recovery will be conducted by the Information Technology
Division. Plans to cover the costs of recovery are included in the Budgeting
and Acquisition section.<br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='margin-top:0in'><a name="_Toc134528018"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>HUMAN RESOURCES</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528019"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Roles and
responsibilities</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc134528020"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Senior
Leadership</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>Continuity Plan activation is a scenario-driven process that allows
flexible, scalable response to all hazards/threats that might disrupt
operations. Continuity Plan activation will not be required for all emergencies
or disruptions.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:6.0pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>The process for activating the continuity plan
has three basic steps:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-top:6.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
4.0pt;margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l24 level1 lfo19;
text-autospace:none'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>(1)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The <span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>division director</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'> </b>is aware of, or is notified, that a disruption to normal
operations is planned, is anticipated, or has occurred.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-top:6.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
4.0pt;margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l24 level1 lfo19;
text-autospace:none'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>(2)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The <span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>division director</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'> </b>evaluates the situation along with its potential, anticipated, or
known effects on agency operations and decides whether to activate the
Continuity Plan.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-top:6.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
4.0pt;margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l24 level1 lfo19;
text-autospace:none'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>(3)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The <span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>division director</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'> </b>initiates the process to inform all employees of the situation and
the actions they should take.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>Based on the type and severity of the emergency, the </span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>Continuity <span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>Plan may be activated by one of the following methods:<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l20 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(1)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
executive director of the TDCJ may initiate agency-wide Continuity activation,
led by the TDCJ Office of Emergency Management.<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l20 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(2)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The TLDD
director, or designated successor, may initiate the Continuity Plan activation
for the division based on an emergency or threat directed at the division.<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l20 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(3)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Local
department supervisors or managers may initiate a partial Continuity Plan
activation for their location based on an emergency or threat directed locally.<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>The decision to activate the </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Continuity<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b><span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>Plan and related actions will be tailored for the situation based on
projected or actual impact. </span></span><b><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#003366'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-top:6.0pt;text-align:center'><b><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#003366'>Decision
Process<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;mso-layout-grid-align:
none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-no-proof:
yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_2" o:spid="_x0000_i1027"
 type="#_x0000_t75" alt="Diagram&#10;&#10;Description automatically generated"
 style='width:432.6pt;height:174.6pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="TLDD%20COOP_files/image005.jpg" o:title="Diagram&#10;&#10;Description automatically generated"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=577 height=233
src="TLDD%20COOP_files/image006.jpg"
alt="Diagram&#10;&#10;Description automatically generated" v:shapes="Picture_x0020_2"><![endif]></span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528021"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>All Personnel</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Every member of the organization
will train and prepare in advance for a continuity <span class=GramE>event</span>
so they are prepared to act quickly<span style='color:black;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'> in an emergency. <span class=GramE>Each individual</span> will also d</span>evelop
a Family Support Plan to increase personal and family preparedness<span
style='color:black;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>. The </span></span><a
href="http://www.ready.gov"><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>www.ready.gov</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat;color:black;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> website provides guidance for developing a Family
Support Plan and includes a Get Ready Now pamphlet that explains the
importance of planning, and a template that can be tailored to meet family-specific
planning requirements.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h4 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Hlk520187134"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Personnel Accountability <o:p></o:p></span></a></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:
none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520187134'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>It is important to account for all personnel during
a continuity event. The<b> </b></span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520187134'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>Personnel Accountability Coordinator<b> </b><span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>will account for personnel using </span>supervisor
call-trees, automated systems, or other available processes<span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>. Accountability information is reported to
the </span>Continuity Director<b> </b><span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>at
</span>one-<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>hour intervals. The process
will continue until all personnel have been accounted for.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:3.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:
none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520187134'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520187134'></span>

<h3 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528022"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Continuity Personnel</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'>The organization has
determined the positions necessary to conduct essential functions, and to
authorize and approve the work. Key positions include </span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>the<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>Continuity
Coordinator, Continuity Team members, senior leadership and their successors,
and others who are assigned continuity responsibilities.</span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'> These individuals will report to the alternate location or other
assigned location. A copy of the current roster is found on the TLDD SharePoint
site in the COOP directory. The <span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>COOP
Coordinator</span> is responsible for maintaining the roster and ensuring
personnel are correctly matched to required positions.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoCaption align=center style='text-align:center;page-break-after:
avoid'><a name="_Toc134526746"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:Montserrat'>Table </span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc134526746'></span><!--[if supportFields]><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Continuity
personnel are responsible for creating and maintaining go kits that are either
pre-positioned at the alternate location, or that they will carry with them
when they go. In order to maintain currency of drive-away kits, TLDD has
established procedures for updating the kits. These procedures include but are
not limited to having Continuity personnel bring kits on annual exercises,
distributing quarterly update materials, and establishing an acquisition
program to regularly replace agency-supplied emergency items. A typical go kit
should contain those items listed in the table below.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;

<h2><a name="_Toc134528023"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Succession and
Delegations of Authority</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>In the event the </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>division
director<b> </b><span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>is rendered incapable
or unavailable to fulfill their duties, successors have been identified to
ensure there is no lapse in decision-making authority. <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><b><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:navy'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
COOP Coordinator<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> is responsible for
ensuring orders of succession are up-to-date, and copies can be found </span></span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>on the TLDD SharePoint site in the COOP directory</span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>. When changes occur,
they will be distributed by the TLDD Office of Information Management.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>When the primary holder of one of these positions, or their acting
successor, becomes unreachable or incapable of performing their duties, the </span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>COOP Director<b> </b><span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>will notify the next successor in line and inform other internal and
external stakeholders of the substitution. <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>Successor training will be conducted
annually, and the dates and topics will be documented by</span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'> <a name="OLE_LINK5"></a><a
name="OLE_LINK6"><span style='mso-bookmark:OLE_LINK5'><span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>the COOP Coordinator</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>and
stored in the Training Database which is an essential record.</span></a></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:OLE_LINK5'></span><span style='mso-bookmark:OLE_LINK6'></span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='margin-top:0in'><a name="_Toc134528024"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>COMMUNICATIONS</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528025"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Resilient Systems</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>The<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>
</b>organization has identified multiple, resilient communication systems,
located at the primary and alternate location(s), and telework or virtual
office location. These systems will</span><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> support the needs of the organization during all hazards/threats.
The organization also maintains communications equipment for use by employees
with disabilities and hearing impairment. During a pandemic, when the limiting
factor is loss of manpower rather than loss of facility or equipment, the
diverse forms of communication can support social distancing efforts. All
communications systems and equipment are maintained by the Information
Technology Division and are made available to agency staff.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528026"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Alert and Notification</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=coltext style='margin:0in;text-align:justify;tab-stops:.5in'><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Montserrat'>I<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>n the event of a potential or actual interruption, </span>the TLDD<span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> will take the following steps to communicate
the organizations operating status:<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l13 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(1)<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>The Continuity Director will notify the TDCJ Office of Emergency
Management of the emergency requiring Continuity <span class=GramE>activation</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l13 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(2)<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>The Continuity Director will determine the extent of Continuity Plan
activation that is appropriate for the affected <span class=GramE>office</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l13 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(3)<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>The Continuity Director will authorize Continuity Personnel to initiate
the Continuity Plan<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l13 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(4)<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>The Continuity Director will continue to provide information and
guidance to the ERG as the critical event evolves and responsive action is <span
class=GramE>required</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l13 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(5)<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>Continuity Personnel will maintain communication with each other and
the Continuity Director during the <span class=GramE>emergency</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l13 level1 lfo7;tab-stops:list .5in'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>(6)<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>TLDD personnel will notify family members, next of kin, and/or
emergency contacts of the Continuity Plan activation, as <span class=GramE>appropriate</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528027"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Tracking the Threat</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>The organization will remain informed of the threat environment using all
available means. </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The COOP Director<span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> will evaluate all available information
relating to:<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:auto;
text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Direction
and guidance from higher <span class=GramE>authorities;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The health
and safety of <span class=GramE>personnel;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The ability
to execute Essential <span class=GramE>Functions;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Changes in
readiness or advisory <span class=GramE>levels;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Intelligence
<span class=GramE>reports;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:
auto;text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
potential or actual effects on communication systems, information systems,
office facilities, and other vital equipment; and,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:.75in;mso-add-space:auto;
text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo12'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
expected duration of the <span class=GramE>emergency situation</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc134528028"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>ALTERNATE LOCATIONS
AND TELEWORK</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528029"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Space and
Infrastructure Summary</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>The alternate location(s) provide the following in
sufficient quantities to sustain operations until normal operations can be
resumed (usually within 30 days):<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Space and
equipment, including computer equipment and software. The alternate location can
accommodate sufficient personnel to maintain EFs. Facility floor plans,
equipment inventory, and <span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>other
applicable documents</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>are <span
class=GramE>available</span> </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'>the TLDD SharePoint site
in the COOP directory</span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Capability
to perform EFs within the RTO. The facility will remain available until normal
operations can be resumed, often within 30 days.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Reliable
logistical support, services, and infrastructure systems. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Consideration
for health, safety, security, and emotional well-being of personnel, including <span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>physical security, fitness activities, access
to the Employee Assistance Program, and presence of security</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:black'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Emergency/back-up
power capability. </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:black'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528030"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Access to Communications, Internet, and Remote Servers</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>The alternate location(s) provides the following
infrastructure to ensure access to primary servers, backup storage, and the
essential records database:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Interoperable
communications, and connections, for effective interaction. Additional
information on continuity communications is found in the Communications section
of this plan.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Capabilities
to access and use Essential Records. Additional information on accessing
Essential Records is found in the Essential Records section of this plan.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Systems and
configurations that are used to complete EFs. IT support at the alternate
location can be accessed through the ITD Help Desk. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528031"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Maps, Directions, Security, and Access</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<h2><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></h2>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528032"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Telework</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'> <o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Continuity
operations will begin at the date and time stated in the plan activation
notification. Within eight hours of plan activation, the IT manager will
determine if the infrastructure in the primary operating facility is accessible
and fully functional. The IT manager will provide personnel with the status of the
agencys infrastructure and identify which IT resources they should use.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Once
continuity operations have begun, all personnel will begin teleworking and
will:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l5 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Contact
their manager by email, text, or telephone to verify their arrival and ability
to telework from their location.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l5 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Upon
notification from the IT manager regarding which IT resources will be used,
login to the appropriate location.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l5 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Report to
their <span class=GramE>manager</span> their ability to access essential
records needed to perform their functions or obstacles they are facing.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l5 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Begin
performing EFs or supporting activities within the RTO.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528033"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>Activation/Relocation</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>Upon activation of the Continuity Plan by </span><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>the COOP Director<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>, EFs may relocate
to the alternate location(s). </span>The Facility Coordinator<span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> will notify the point of contact at the
alternate location(s) of the activation and need to occupy the space and ensure
that the continuity operations can begin within the RTO. <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>If <span class=GramE>the</span> emergency occurs <u>during work hours</u>
continuity activities will be implemented as follows.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0in' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Advance Team and
     Continuity Team members will deploy to the designated alternate location
     from the primary facility or their current location.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Non-continuity
     personnel will receive instructions from </span><span style='font-family:
     Montserrat'>the Personnel Accountability Coordinator<span
     style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>. In most situations they will be
     directed to return home to await further instructions. <o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Information will
     be provided regarding safety precautions and clear routes to use when
     leaving the primary operating facility.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>If the emergency occurs <u>during non-work hours</u> continuity
activities will be implemented as follows:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0in' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Advance Team and
     Continuity Team members will deploy to the designated alternate location
     from their current location.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Non-continuity
     personnel will remain at their residence or other designated <span
     class=GramE>location, but</span> must be prepared to replace or augment
     continuity personnel within </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>one
     hour<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> of notification, or as
     advised. Staff replacements will be coordinated by the </span>Personnel
     Accountability Coordinator<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>.<o:p></o:p></span></span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:12.0pt;text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:
none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>Non-continuity personnel may be required to replace or augment continuity
personnel during activation and should remain available as instructed. These
activities will be coordinated by the </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Personnel
Accountability Coordinator<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>. <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>The advance team should arrive and prepare the alternate location(s) for
use so that continuity operations can be resumed within the RTO. The advance
team will:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0in' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Ensure infrastructure
     systems, such as power and heating, ventilating, and air conditioning are
     functional.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Prepare check-in
     duty stations for the Continuity Teams arrival.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Address telephone
     inquiries from continuity and non-continuity staff.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Address any other
     needs as identified.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>In-processing procedures include </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>briefing
on the Continuity Plan and the situation where appropriate, collection of
contact information, appropriate notifications as needed, assignment of
workspaces and resources, and any training or orientation needed.<span
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><i><span style='font-family:Montserrat;color:#002060'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></i></b></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc134528034"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>RECONSTITUTION</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528035"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Procedures</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Within </span><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>24
hours<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> of an emergency relocation, and
after receiving approval from the appropriate state and </span></span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>local law enforcement and emergency
services</span><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
the Reconstitution Team will initiate and coordinate operations to salvage,
restore, and recover the primary operating facility and resources</span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

  minor-latin'>TLDD<span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'> is fully capable of

<p class=MsoTitleCxSpLast><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Continuity
Program Management<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

</span>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:16.0pt;
font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:Times;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;
color:#2F5496;mso-themecolor:accent1;mso-themeshade:191;mso-font-kerning:16.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<h1 style='margin-top:0in;text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528036"><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>TRAINING, TESTING, AND EXERCISING (TT&amp;E)</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
organization<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>participates in the
full spectrum of readiness and preparedness activities to ensure personnel can
continue EFs in an all-hazard/threat environment. The readiness activities are
divided into two key areas: <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0in' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Organizational
     readiness and preparedness<o:p></o:p></span></li>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo3;
     tab-stops:list .5in;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
     style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>Staff readiness
     and preparedness<o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Hlk520186699"><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>In addition, the<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'> </b>organization<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>conducts
the following continuity readiness and preparedness activities:<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b><span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
bold'>orientation training, brown bags or working lunch informational sessions,
and senior management addresses to the organization regarding continuity, among
others</span>. <o:p></o:p></span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>The<b> </b>organization
has established a</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'> TT&amp;E program to support preparedness and
validate continuity capabilities during any disruption of operations. It is
essential to demonstrate, assess, and improve the ability to execute the
continuity program procedures.<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>All
continuity TT&amp;E events are documented, including the <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l2 level1 lfo10;text-autospace:none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:black'>Event date, <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l2 level1 lfo10;text-autospace:none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:black'>Event type, <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l2 level1 lfo10;text-autospace:none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:black'>Participants<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l2 level1 lfo10;text-autospace:none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:black'>Test results, <o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l2 level1 lfo10;text-autospace:none'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:black'>Feedback forms, participant questionnaires, and other
documents resulting from the event.<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>Documentation
is managed by the <span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>COOP Coordinator</span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>and is found </span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'>on the TLDD SharePoint
site in the COOP directory.<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></p>

<span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk520186699'></span>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528037"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Training</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Awareness
Training for All Personnel<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.25in;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>The goal of awareness training is to familiarize
all personnel with the organization's continuity of operations plan (COOP).
This training covers the following topics:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l7 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>a.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Introduction
to COOP: Explain the purpose and importance of having a COOP in place,
emphasizing the need to ensure uninterrupted delivery of essential services
during emergencies.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l7 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>b.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Individual
Roles and Responsibilities: Outline the specific roles and responsibilities of
each staff member in the context of the COOP, ensuring everyone understands
their part in maintaining operational continuity.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l7 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>c.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Communication
Protocols: Review the communication channels and procedures to be followed during
an emergency, including reporting structures, emergency contact information,
and methods for disseminating important updates.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l7 level1 lfo24'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>d.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Evacuation
and Shelter-in-Place Procedures: Train staff on evacuation routes and
shelter-in-place procedures, ensuring everyone knows what to do in the event of
an emergency.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Cross
Training for Continuity, Reconstitution, and Devolution Staff<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.25in;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>Cross-training aims to ensure that key personnel
are familiar with the responsibilities of others in their team and can step in
when needed. The training should cover the following areas:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>a.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Core
Functions and Responsibilities: Provide detailed information on the roles and
duties of continuity, reconstitution, and devolution staff to ensure smooth
transitions during an emergency.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>b.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Inter-team
Collaboration: Emphasize the importance of working closely with other teams
within the organization, sharing knowledge and resources as needed.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>c.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Backup
Systems and Processes: Train staff on using backup systems and implementing
alternative processes during an emergency, ensuring the continuity of
operations.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l10 level1 lfo25'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>d.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Scenario-based
Training: Conduct exercises and simulations to practice responding to various
emergency situations, helping staff build confidence in their ability to carry
out their roles under pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Succession
Training<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.25in;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'>Succession training focuses on preparing staff
to assume higher-level roles and responsibilities in the event of key personnel
absences. This training should cover:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l23 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>a.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Leadership
Skills Development: Equip staff with the necessary skills to effectively lead a
team, including decision-making, communication, and conflict resolution.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l23 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>b.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Understanding
of Key Roles: Provide in-depth information on the roles and responsibilities of
key personnel, enabling staff to step in as needed during an emergency.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l23 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>c.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Risk
Management: Train staff on identifying and mitigating potential risks and
threats to the organization, helping them make informed decisions during
emergencies.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='text-align:justify;text-indent:-.25in;
mso-list:l23 level1 lfo26'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-fareast-font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Montserrat'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>d.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Policy and
Procedure Review: Ensure staff are familiar with the organization's policies
and procedures related to the COOP, enabling them to make decisions in line
with organizational guidelines.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in'><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Montserrat;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;color:#002060'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528038"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Testing and Exercises</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<div align=center>

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><span

  style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:2;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-2.7pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>Training:</span></b><span style='font-family:
  Montserrat'> Have those individuals with continuity roles and
  responsibilities received continuity training?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-right-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.15pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>All
  individuals with continuity roles and responsibilities, including leadership
  and the planning team, have received continuity training. The continuity
  planners/managers have received advanced training, such as achieving their
  FEMA Level I and Level II Continuity Practitioner certificate.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:3;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-2.7pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>Exercising:</span></b><span style='font-family:
  Montserrat'> Has the organization identified and incorporated the results
  from previous exercises and real-world events to guide the development of the
  continuity program?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  organization used results from all previous exercises and real-world events
  to guide current planning efforts.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:4;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  </td>

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Building</span><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:5;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-2.7pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>Training:</span></b><span style='font-family:
  Montserrat'> Have all staff members completed continuity awareness training?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 2.25pt;

  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.15pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>All
  required staff completed awareness training on the continuity plan and roles,
  responsibilities, and expectations upon its activation. <o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:6;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-2.7pt;margin-bottom:

  style='font-family:Montserrat'>Training:</span></b><span style='font-family:
  Montserrat'> Has the organization trained continuity personnel on continuity
  plans and strategies?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:
