  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.15pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>All
  primary and alternate continuity personnel, to include leadership and/or
  elected officials, have received up-to-date training.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:7;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-2.7pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>Training:</span></b><span style='font-family:
  Montserrat'> Has continuity personnel participated in regular continuity
  training activities with other continuity programs (both internally and
  externally)?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-right-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.15pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
  organization trained all continuity planning team members on other inter- and
  intra-organizational continuity programs.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:8;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-2.7pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>Exercising:</span></b><span style='font-family:
  Montserrat'> Has the organization conducted testing of alert and notification
  procedures?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-right-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:-1.15pt;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>The
  organization tests alert and notification procedures and implemented
  improvement action planning. Testing demonstrated an improvement compared to
  previous tests.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:9;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Exercising:</span></b><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'> Has the organization conducted testing of
  activation procedures?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><span

  and implemented improvement action planning. Testing demonstrated an
  improvement compared to previous tests.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

  over a multi-year period.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:5;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Exercising:</span></b><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'> Has the organization conducted regular
  testing of critical systems and equipment and strategies to meet associated recovery
  time objectives?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-right-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>The organization tested recovery time
  objectives for critical systems and equipment within the past year by
  incorporating the test into an organization-wide exercise. Testing occurs at
  least annually over a multi-year period.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:6;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  solid #003366 2.25pt;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Exercising:</span></b><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'> Has the organization regularly conducted
  organization-wide continuity exercises?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid #003366 1.0pt;border-right:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-right-alt:solid #003366 2.25pt;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><span
  style='font-family:Montserrat'>The organization, including senior leadership,
  exercised the comprehensive continuity plan in a functional or full-scale
  exercise within the past year and annually over a multi-year period.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:7;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  mso-border-top-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid #003366 .5pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><b

  style='font-family:Montserrat'> Has the organization progressively exercised
  its continuity plan and procedures?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><span

  full-scale exercise of its continuity plan within the past year.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:8;page-break-inside:avoid'>
  <td width=280 valign=top style='width:210.35pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0in;text-align:justify'><b

  style='font-family:Montserrat'> Has the organization conducted exercises of
  the reconstitution plan or procedures to exercise recovery from the effects
  of an emergency and transitioning back to normal operations after continuity
  plan activation?<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=386 valign=top style='width:289.5pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>

  exercised the reconstitution plan in a functional or full-scale exercise
  within the past two years and biennially over a multi-year period.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>

<h2 style='text-align:justify'><a name="_Toc134528039"><span style='font-family:
Montserrat'>After-Action Evaluation and Improvement Planning</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>A comprehensive debriefing or hot wash
is conducted after each exercise, allowing participants to identify weaknesses
in plans and procedures and recommend revisions to the organizations continuity
plan. Documentation from TT&amp;E hot washes is found </span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>on the TLDD SharePoint site in the COOP directory</span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:black'>A corrective action plan (CAP) is
completed to document and prioritize issues identified during TT&amp;E
activities, assessments, and emergency operations. The CAP incorporates
evaluations, after action reviews (AARs), and lessons learned. CAP is
maintained by the <span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>COOP Coordinator</span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> </b>and documentation is found </span><span
style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:
italic'>on the TLDD SharePoint site in the COOP directory.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-style:italic'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

avoid'><a name="_Toc134526752"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;

<h1><a name="_Toc134528040"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>APPENDIX A:
LIST OF SUPPORT APPENDICES</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:Montserrat;background:lightgrey;
mso-highlight:lightgrey'>Insert Continuity Plan specific appendices here. Such
as:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:

<h1><a name="_Toc134528043"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>APPENDIX D: PLAN
MAINTENANCE</span></a><span style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<h2><a name="_Toc134528044"><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Annual Review</span></a><span
style='font-family:Montserrat'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial'>Once a year, <span style='mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>the TLDD</span> reviews
its Continuity Plan, components, and supporting elements, and makes any
required updates or changes.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;mso-layout-grid-align:none;
text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:Montserrat;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Develop
  a Continuity of Operations Plan (COOP) that addresses the identified risks
  and outlines strategies for maintaining essential functions during an
  emergency.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-family:Montserrat'>Monitor
  potential threats and hazards, such as severe weather, public health
  emergencies, or geopolitical events, and adjust preparedness activities
  accordingly.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

  <td width=67 style='width:50.05pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
